DESCRIPTION: GridBox in a table
EXPECTED:
  text[System`InputForm]: TableForm[{{a, b}, {c, d}}]
  text[System`OutputForm]: a   b

c   d

  text[System`StandardForm]: a   b

c   d

  text[System`TraditionalForm]: a   b

c   d

  latex[System`InputForm]: \text{TableForm[\{\{a, b\}, \{c, d\}\}]}
  latex[System`OutputForm]: \text{a   b\newline
\newline
c   d\newline
}
  latex[System`StandardForm]: \begin{array}{cc} a & b\\ c & d\end{array}
  latex[System`TraditionalForm]: \begin{array}{cc} a & b\\ c & d\end{array}
  mathml[System`InputForm]: <mtext>TableForm[{{a,&nbsp;b},&nbsp;{c,&nbsp;d}}]</mtext>
  mathml[System`OutputForm]: <mtext>a&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;b<mspace linebreak="newline" /><mspace linebreak="newline" />c&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;d<mspace linebreak="newline" /></mtext>
  mathml[System`StandardForm]: <mtable columnalign="center">
 <mtr>
  <mtd columnalign="center">
   <mi>a</mi>
  </mtd>
  <mtd columnalign="center">
   <mi>b</mi>
  </mtd>
 </mtr>
 <mtr>
  <mtd columnalign="center">
   <mi>c</mi>
  </mtd>
  <mtd columnalign="center">
   <mi>d</mi>
  </mtd>
 </mtr>
</mtable>
  mathml[System`TraditionalForm]: <mtable columnalign="center">
 <mtr>
  <mtd columnalign="center">
   <mi>a</mi>
  </mtd>
  <mtd columnalign="center">
   <mi>b</mi>
  </mtd>
 </mtr>
 <mtr>
  <mtd columnalign="center">
   <mi>c</mi>
  </mtd>
  <mtd columnalign="center">
   <mi>d</mi>
  </mtd>
 </mtr>
</mtable>
---

FILE: test/format/format_tests.yaml
INPUT: a^(g[b]/c)
DESCRIPTION: SuperscriptBox with a nested expression.
EXPECTED:
  text[System`InputForm]: a^(g[b]/c)
  text[System`OutputForm]: a ^ (g[b] / c)
  text[System`StandardForm]: a^((g[b]) / c)
  text[System`TraditionalForm]: a^((g(b)) / c)
  latex[System`InputForm]: \text{a${}^{\wedge}$(g[b]/c)}
  latex[System`OutputForm]: \text{a ${}^{\wedge}$ (g[b] / c)}
  latex[System`StandardForm]: a^{\frac{g[b]}{c}}
  latex[System`TraditionalForm]: a^{\frac{g(b)}{c}}
  mathml[System`InputForm]: <mtext>a^(g[b]/c)</mtext>
  mathml[System`OutputForm]: <mtext>a&nbsp;^&nbsp;(g[b]&nbsp;/&nbsp;c)</mtext>
  mathml[System`TraditionalForm]: <msup>
 <mi>a</mi>
 <mfrac>
  <mrow>
   <mi>g</mi>
   <mo>(</mo>
   <mi>b</mi>
   <mo>)</mo>
  </mrow>
  <mi>c</mi>
 </mfrac>
</msup>
---
FILE: test/format/format_tests.yaml

  text[System`StandardForm]: a^4
  text[System`TraditionalForm]: a^4
  latex[System`InputForm]: \text{a${}^{\wedge}$4}
  latex[System`OutputForm]: \text{a ${}^{\wedge}$ 4}
  latex[System`StandardForm]: a^4
  latex[System`TraditionalForm]: a^4
  mathml[System`InputForm]: <mtext>a^4</mtext>
  mathml[System`OutputForm]: <mtext>a&nbsp;^&nbsp;4</mtext>
  mathml[System`StandardForm]: <msup>
 <mi>a</mi>
 <mn>4</mn>
</msup>
  mathml[System`TraditionalForm]: <msup>
 <mi>a</mi>
 <mn>4</mn>
</msup>

FILE: test/format/format_tests.yaml
INPUT: Optional[x__, a+b]
DESCRIPTION: Optional with two arguments

  text[System`StandardForm]: x__:a+b

  latex[System`StandardForm]: \text{x\_\_}:a+b
  mathml[System`OutputForm]: <mtext>x__&nbsp;:&nbsp;a&nbsp;+&nbsp;b</mtext>

FILE: test/format/format_tests.yaml
INPUT: a+PrecedenceForm[b+c,10]
DESCRIPTION: PrecedenceForm
EXPECTED:
  text[System`InputForm]: a + (PrecedenceForm[b + c, 10])
  text[System`OutputForm]: a + (b + c)
  text[System`StandardForm]: a+(b+c)
  text[System`TraditionalForm]: a+(b+c)
  latex[System`OutputForm]: \text{a + (b + c)}
  latex[System`StandardForm]: a+(b+c)
  mathml[System`OutputForm]: <mtext>a&nbsp;+&nbsp;(b&nbsp;+&nbsp;c)</mtext>
  mathml[System`StandardForm]: <mrow>
 <mi>a</mi>
 <mo>+</mo>
 <mrow>
  <mo>(</mo>
  <mrow>
   <mi>b</mi>
   <mo>+</mo>
   <mi>c</mi>
  </mrow>
  <mo>)</mo>
 </mrow>
</mrow>
